// Needs map npcland



npcland,99,93,4	script	Npcland Manager	435,{

if(#Completed <=0){ set #Completed,0;}
if(#quest <=0){ set #quest,0;}
if(#Daily <=0){ set #Daily,0;}
if($Reset <=0){ set $Reset,0;}

if(getgmlevel() > 10){
	mes "^DC143C[Npcland Manager]^000000";
	mes "Yes, Game Master?";
	next;
	switch(select("Goto npc","Quit","Debug-> Viewpoint Check","Debug-> Change weekly word (GM lvl80+)","Debug-> View weekly word (GM lvl80+)")){
		case 1:
			goto Npcland_Main;
		case 2:
			goto Npcland_Quit;
		case 3:
			goto Npcland_Debug;
		case 4:
			goto Npcland_WordChange;
		case 5:
			goto Npcland_WordCheck;
    		}
	}


Npcland_Main:
	if($Reset==1){ mes "PLEASE NOTE: The weekly word was changed by a GM recently!";
	next;}
	mes "^DC143C[Npcland Manager]^000000";
	mes "Hello "+strcharinfo(0)+" and welcome to Npcland! Here I'm running a weekly event.";

	menu "Start today's quest",Npcland_Start,"Enter today's letter",Npcland_Letter,"Enter weekly word",Npcland_WeekCheck,"Missed weekly reward",Npcland_NoWeeklyCheck,"Information",Npcland_Info,"Reset Daily Quest",Npcland_Reset,"Im stuck between npcs",Npcland_Stuck,"Get me outta here!",Npcland_WarpAway,"Quit",Npcland_Quit;



Npcland_Start:
	if(gettime(4)==1 && #Daily==1) goto Npcland_mdk;
	if(gettime(4)==2 && #Daily==2) goto Npcland_mdk;
	if(gettime(4)==3 && #Daily==3) goto Npcland_mdk;
	if(gettime(4)==4 && #Daily==4) goto Npcland_mdk;
	if(gettime(4)==5 && #Daily==5) goto Npcland_mdk;
	if(gettime(4)==6 && #Daily==6) goto Npcland_mdk;

	if(#Daily==6){ mes "^DC143C[Npcland Manager]^000000";
	mes "Im sorry but you are already at 6 Dailys. You must redeem your prize for the week!";
	close;}

	if($Letter==7){ mes "^DC143C[Npcland Manager]^000000";
	mes "Im sorry but today is Sunday and there are no quests on Sundays";
	close;}

Npcland_Stuck:
	mes "^DC143C[Npcland Manager]^000000";
	mes "This feature allows you to go back to your previous npc and continue on...IF, you remember the last 1 you talked to. If you dont, I suggest you just use the reset feature.";
	next;
	mes "^DC143C[Npcland Manager]^000000";
	mes "Do you wish to backtrack to your previous npc?";
	menu "Yes",Npcland_YesStuck,"No, Ill pass",Npcland_Main;


Npcland_YesStuck:
	next;
	if(#quest==0) goto Npcland_mdk;
	if(gettime(4)==1 && #Daily==1) goto Npcland_mdk;
	if(gettime(4)==2 && #Daily==2) goto Npcland_mdk;
	if(gettime(4)==3 && #Daily==3) goto Npcland_mdk;
	if(gettime(4)==4 && #Daily==4) goto Npcland_mdk;

	if(gettime(4)==6 && #Daily==6) goto Npcland_mdk;
	if(gettime(4)==0) goto Npcland_mdk;
	if(#Week==1) goto Npcland_mdk;

	if(#Last_Day==gettime(4)) goto npcland_mdk;

//#quest,#quest+1 variables to facilitate cheaters tryin to input daily letter more than once
	if($Dletter$=="R" && #quest==17) goto Npcland_mdk;

	if($Dletter$=="R" && #quest==17) goto Npcland_mdk;

	if($Dletter$=="B" && #quest==18) goto Npcland_mdk;

	if($Dletter$=="M" && #quest==14) goto Npcland_mdk;
	if($Dletter$=="I" && #quest==12) goto Npcland_mdk;
	if($Dletter$=="T" && #quest==12) goto Npcland_mdk;

	if($Dletter$=="R" && #quest==17) goto Npcland_mdk;

	if($Dletter$=="G" && #quest==18) goto Npcland_mdk;
	if($Dletter$=="H" && #quest==16) goto Npcland_mdk;

	if($Dletter$=="I" && #quest==12) goto Npcland_mdk;
	if($Dletter$=="E" && #quest==20) goto Npcland_mdk;
	if($Dletter$=="S" && #quest==14) goto Npcland_mdk;

	if($Dletter$=="Z" && #quest==16) goto Npcland_mdk;
	if($Dletter$=="A" && #quest==18) goto Npcland_mdk;

	if($Dletter$=="V" && #quest==12) goto Npcland_mdk;
	if($Dletter$=="I" && #quest==12) goto Npcland_mdk;
	if($Dletter$=="C" && #quest==11) goto Npcland_mdk;
	if($Dletter$=="E" && #quest==20) goto Npcland_mdk;

	if($Dletter$=="D" && #quest==19) goto Npcland_mdk;

	if($Dletter$=="N" && #quest==18) goto Npcland_mdk;
	if($Dletter$=="C" && #quest==11) goto Npcland_mdk;
	if($Dletter$=="E" && #quest==20) goto Npcland_mdk;
	if($Dletter$=="R" && #quest==17) goto Npcland_mdk;
//end of #quest,#quest+1 variables
	else set #quest,#quest-1;
	mes "^DC143C[Npcland Manager]^000000";
	mes "Done, now go talk to the last npc you were told to";
	goto Npcland_Quit;


Npcland_Info:
	mes "^DC143C[Npcland Manager]^000000";
	mes "This is a weeklong event that takes a bit of patience. Each day I direct you to various npcs. Each npc directs you to the next.";
	next;
	mes "^DC143C[Npcland Manager]^000000";
	mes "You will see your minimap light up. Those lights will spell a certain letter that you need to remember. Once you have talked to the required npcs, you come back to me.";
	next;
	mes "^DC143C[Npcland Manager]^000000";
	mes "You will then give me the letter that was displayed on the map. If its correct, you will gain a prize. If not, then take another look at your minimap and try again.";
	next;
	mes "^DC143C[Npcland Manager]^000000";
	mes "Be sure to keep track of your letters! These will be needed near the end of the week. On every Saturday I will ask you to tell me the word that you have formed.";
	next;
	mes "^DC143C[Npcland Manager]^000000";
	mes "If you are correct, you will win an even greater prize...otherwise, you will lose out on the prize.";
	next;
	mes "^DC143C[Npcland Manager]^000000";
	mes "GMs have the ability to change the weekly word, but it will be announced serverwide. If the word is changed, you will miss out on the weekly reward however...";
	next;
	mes "^DC143C[Npcland Manager]^000000";
	mes "You will receive something for your efforts in exchange. You will be rewarded based on how many daily quests you complete if you miss out on the weekly reward.";
	next;
	mes "^DC143C[Npcland Manager]^000000";
	mes "1 daily  = 100k zeny";
	mes "2 dailys = 250k zeny";
	mes "3 dailys = 500k zeny";
	mes "4 dailys = 1 OCA";
	mes "5 dailys = Random 1-10 OPB";
	next;
	mes "^DC143C[Npcland Manager]^000000";
	mes "And if you so happen to do all 6 daily quests but cant remember the previous letters, then you shall receive 1 Bloody Branch for your efforts. So either way...you win!";
	next;
	mes "^DC143C[Npcland Manager]^000000";

	next;
	mes "^DC143C[Npcland Manager]^000000";
	mes "I am now returning you to the main menu...";
	next;
	goto Npcland_Main;

	else if($Letter==6 && #quest==15 && $Word$=="BSMITH") goto Npcland_DailyCheck;

	else if($Letter==1 && #quest==16 && $Word$=="RANGER") goto Npcland_DailyCheck;
	else if($Letter==2 && #quest==17 && $Word$=="RANGER") goto Npcland_DailyCheck;
	else if($Letter==3 && #quest==17 && $Word$=="RANGER") goto Npcland_DailyCheck;
	else if($Letter==4 && #quest==17 && $Word$=="RANGER") goto Npcland_DailyCheck;
	else if($Letter==5 && #quest==19 && $Word$=="RANGER") goto Npcland_DailyCheck;
	else if($Letter==6 && #quest==16 && $Word$=="RANGER") goto Npcland_DailyCheck;

	else if($Letter==1 && #quest==17 && $Word$=="AMISTR") goto Npcland_DailyCheck;
	else if($Letter==2 && #quest==13 && $Word$=="AMISTR") goto Npcland_DailyCheck;
	else if($Letter==3 && #quest==11 && $Word$=="AMISTR") goto Npcland_DailyCheck;
	else if($Letter==4 && #quest==13 && $Word$=="AMISTR") goto Npcland_DailyCheck;
	else if($Letter==5 && #quest==11 && $Word$=="AMISTR") goto Npcland_DailyCheck;
	else if($Letter==6 && #quest==16 && $Word$=="AMISTR") goto Npcland_DailyCheck;

	else if($Letter==1 && #quest==14 && $Word$=="KNIGHT") goto Npcland_DailyCheck;
	else if($Letter==2 && #quest==17 && $Word$=="KNIGHT") goto Npcland_DailyCheck;
	else if($Letter==3 && #quest==11 && $Word$=="KNIGHT") goto Npcland_DailyCheck;
	else if($Letter==4 && #quest==17 && $Word$=="KNIGHT") goto Npcland_DailyCheck;
	else if($Letter==5 && #quest==15 && $Word$=="KNIGHT") goto Npcland_DailyCheck;
	else if($Letter==6 && #quest==11 && $Word$=="KNIGHT") goto Npcland_DailyCheck;

	else if($Letter==1 && #quest==13 && $Word$=="PRIEST") goto Npcland_DailyCheck;
	else if($Letter==2 && #quest==16 && $Word$=="PRIEST") goto Npcland_DailyCheck;
	else if($Letter==3 && #quest==11 && $Word$=="PRIEST") goto Npcland_DailyCheck;
	else if($Letter==4 && #quest==19 && $Word$=="PRIEST") goto Npcland_DailyCheck;
	else if($Letter==5 && #quest==13 && $Word$=="PRIEST") goto Npcland_DailyCheck;
	else if($Letter==6 && #quest==11 && $Word$=="PRIEST") goto Npcland_DailyCheck;

	else if($Letter==1 && #quest==11 && $Word$=="WIZARD") goto Npcland_DailyCheck;
	else if($Letter==2 && #quest==11 && $Word$=="WIZARD") goto Npcland_DailyCheck;
	else if($Letter==3 && #quest==15 && $Word$=="WIZARD") goto Npcland_DailyCheck;
	else if($Letter==4 && #quest==17 && $Word$=="WIZARD") goto Npcland_DailyCheck;
	else if($Letter==5 && #quest==16 && $Word$=="WIZARD") goto Npcland_DailyCheck;
	else if($Letter==6 && #quest==18 && $Word$=="WIZARD") goto Npcland_DailyCheck;

	else if($Letter==1 && #quest==17 && $Word$=="NOVICE") goto Npcland_DailyCheck;
	else if($Letter==2 && #quest==16 && $Word$=="NOVICE") goto Npcland_DailyCheck;
	else if($Letter==3 && #quest==11 && $Word$=="NOVICE") goto Npcland_DailyCheck;
	else if($Letter==4 && #quest==11 && $Word$=="NOVICE") goto Npcland_DailyCheck;
	else if($Letter==5 && #quest==10 && $Word$=="NOVICE") goto Npcland_DailyCheck;
	else if($Letter==6 && #quest==19 && $Word$=="NOVICE") goto Npcland_DailyCheck;

	else if($Letter==1 && #quest==18 && $Word$=="DANCER") goto Npcland_DailyCheck;
	else if($Letter==2 && #quest==17 && $Word$=="DANCER") goto Npcland_DailyCheck;
	else if($Letter==3 && #quest==17 && $Word$=="DANCER") goto Npcland_DailyCheck;
	else if($Letter==4 && #quest==10 && $Word$=="DANCER") goto Npcland_DailyCheck;
	else if($Letter==5 && #quest==19 && $Word$=="DANCER") goto Npcland_DailyCheck;
	else if($Letter==6 && #quest==16 && $Word$=="DANCER") goto Npcland_DailyCheck;
	if(gettime(4)==0) {goto Npcland_SundayCheck;}
	mes "^DC143C[Npcland Manager]^000000";
	mes "I'm sorry but you havent talked to the required npcs yet. Do you wish to start over todays quest?";
	menu "Restart Quest",Npcland_Reset,"No, Ill try backtracking",Npcland_Quit;


Npcland_WarpAway:
	mes "^DC143C[Npcland Manager]^000000";
	mes "Fine, I shall warp you to your save point...";
	close2;
	warp "SavePoint",0,0;
	end;


Npcland_DailyCheck:
	if(gettime(4)==0){ goto Npcland_SundayCheck;}
	if(gettime(4)==1 && #Daily==1){ goto Npcland_mdk;}
	if(gettime(4)==2 && #Daily==2){ goto Npcland_mdk;}
	if(gettime(4)==3 && #Daily==3){ goto Npcland_mdk;}
	if(gettime(4)==4 && #Daily==4){ goto Npcland_mdk;}
	if(gettime(4)==5 && #Daily==5){ goto Npcland_mdk;}
	if(gettime(4)==6 && #Daily==6){ goto Npcland_mdk;}
	mes "^DC143C[Npcland Manager]^000000";
	mes "Please input your letter...";
	mes "NOTE: You must use capital letters";
	callfunc "Daily Letter";
	input .Letter$;
	if(.Letter$==$Dletter$){ set #Daily,#Daily+1; 
	goto Npcland_Daily;}
	else mes "^DC143C[Npcland Manager]^000000";
	mes "Im sorry but your guess is incorrect...Better luck next time";
	goto Npcland_Quit;


Npcland_Daily:
	next;
	mes "^DC143C[Npcland Manager]^000000";
	mes "Congrats, you win some Zeny";
	set Zeny, Zeny+100000; //100k zeny
	set #Completed,#Completed+1;
	set #quest,#quest+1;
	set #Last_Day,gettime(4);
	callfunc "ViewRemovals";
	next;
	mes "^DC143C[Npcland Manager]^000000";
	mes "Wait, I almost forgot to tell you. Be sure to play everyday. At the end of the week, there is an even bigger prize and make sure to keep track of your letters.";
	if(#Completed==25 || #Completed==50 || #Completed==75 || #Completed==100) goto Npcland_Incentives;
	close;


Npcland_Incentives:
	next;
	mes "^DC143C[Npcland Manager]^000000";
	mes "You thought I was done, didnt you? For completing "+#Completed+" daily quests, you shall receive a bonus for your dedication and hardwork.";
	if(#Completed==25){ getitem 616,5;} // old card albums
	if(#Completed==50){ getitem 607,50;} // ygg berries
	if(#Completed==75){ getitem 12103,5;} //bloody branch
	if(#Completed==100){ getitem 17015,1; // event boxs or something of good value and possibly do a rand(10) with 10 different prizes of decent value for a player since its 100 quests youve done and put in all that effort. valk gear, donation points/cash points, KCP/kafra points, 
	set #Completed,0;}
	next;
	mes "^DC143C[Npcland Manager]^000000";
	mes "I hope you enjoy your gift(s). Thanks for playing...";
	close;


Npcland_WeekCheck:
	//if(gettime(4)==0){ goto Npcland_SundayCheck;}
	if(#Week==1){ goto Npcland_mdk;}
	if(gettime(4)<=5){ goto Npcland_mdk;}
	mes "^DC143C[Npcland Manager]^000000";
	mes "Please input your word";
	mes "NOTE: You must use capital letters";
	input .WWord$;
	if (.WWord$==$Word$) goto Npcland_Weekly;
	else mes "^DC143C[Npcland Manager]^000000";
	mes "Im sorry but you are incorrect. Do you wish to try inputting your word again?";
	menu "Yes, I do",Npcland_WeekCheck,"I give up",Npcland_Quit;


Npcland_NoWeeklyCheck:
	mes "^DC143C[Npcland Manager]^000000";
	mes "Here you can still claim a prize if you havent completed the 6 daily quests, but be warned...Once using this option, you will no longer be able to participate in the rest of the weeks events.";
	next;
	mes "^DC143C[Npcland Manager]^000000";
	mes "Do you wish to claim a prize ending this weeks events for you?";
	menu "Yes",Npcland_NoWeekly,"No",Npcland_Quit;


Npcland_NoWeekly:
	next;
	//if(gettime(4)<=5){ goto Npcland_MissWCheck;}
	if(#week==1){ goto Npcland_mdk;}
	if(#Daily==0){ goto Npcland_mdk;}
	if(#Daily==1){ mes "^DC143C[Npcland Manager]^000000";
	mes "For completing 1 daily quest, you get another 100k zeny";
	set Zeny,Zeny+100000;
	set #Week,1;}
	if(#Daily==2){ 	mes "^DC143C[Npcland Manager]^000000";
	mes "For completing 2 daily quests, you get 250k zeny";
	set Zeny,Zeny+250000;
	set #Week,1;}
	if(#Daily==3){ 	mes "^DC143C[Npcland Manager]^000000";
	mes "For completing 3 daily quests, you get 500k zeny";
	set Zeny,Zeny+500000;
	set #Week,1;}
	if(#Daily==4){ 	mes "^DC143C[Npcland Manager]^000000";
	mes "For completing 4 daily quests, you get 1 OCA";
	getitem 616,1;
	set #Week,1;}
	if(#Daily==5){ 	mes "^DC143C[Npcland Manager]^000000";
	mes "For completing 5 daily quests, you get a random 1-10 Old Purple Boxes";
	getitem 617,rand(10);
	set #Week,1;}
	if(#Daily==6){ mes "^DC143C[Npcland Manager]^000000";
	mes "For completing 6 daily quests and missing out on the weekly prize, you shall receive 1 Bloody Branch";
	getitem 12103,1;
	set #Week,1;}
	next;
	mes "^DC143C[Npcland Manager]^000000";
	mes "Thanks for playing, better luck next week.";
	close;


Npcland_MissWCheck:
	mes "^DC143C[Npcland Manager]^000000";
	mes "Im sorry but this feature is only allowed to be used on Saturday";
	next;
	goto Npcland_Quit;


Npcland_SundayCheck:
	mes "^DC143C[Npcland Manager]^000000";
	mes "Im sorry "+strcharinfo(0)+" but today is Sunday. The deadline for entering your guesses is on Saturday. Sorry for the inconvenience";
	next;
	goto Npcland_Quit;


Npcland_SundayGMChange:
	mes "^DC143C[Npcland Manager]^000000";
	mes "Im sorry "+strcharinfo(0)+" but attempting to change the weekly word on a sunday will cause errors. Im now returning you to the main menu.";
	next;
	goto Npcland_Main;


Npcland_Weekly:
	mes "^DC143C[Npcland Manager]^000000";
	mes "Congratulations for completing this weeks quest! Here is your reward.";
	getitem 17015,1; //make it a eventbox or something like that since it takes a week for this prize
	mes "I wish you goodluck for next weeks quest.";
	set #Week,1;
	close;


Npcland_Quit:
	next;
	mes "^DC143C[Npcland Manager]^000000";
	mes "Seeya...";
	close;


Npcland_Reset:
	next;
	mes "^DC143C[Npcland Manager]^000000";
	mes "Are you sure that you want to remove the minimap markings and reset todays quest? THIS IS YOUR ONLY WARNING!";
	switch(select("Yes","No")){
		case 1:
			next;
			if(#Daily==1 && gettime(4)==1) goto Npcland_mdk;
			if(#Daily==2 && gettime(4)==2) goto Npcland_mdk;
			if(#Daily==3 && gettime(4)==3) goto Npcland_mdk;
			if(#Daily==4 && gettime(4)==4) goto Npcland_mdk;
			if(#Daily==5 && gettime(4)==5) goto Npcland_mdk;
			if(#Daily==6 && gettime(4)==6) goto Npcland_mdk;
			if(#Week==1) goto Npcland_mdk;

			if(#Last_Day==gettime(4)) goto npcland_mdk;

//#quest,#quest+1 variables to facilitate cheaters tryin to input daily letter more than once
			if($Dletter$=="R" && #quest==17) goto Npcland_mdk;
			if($Dletter$=="I" && #quest==12) goto Npcland_mdk;
			if($Dletter$=="V" && #quest==12) goto Npcland_mdk;
			if($Dletter$=="A" && #quest==18) goto Npcland_mdk;
			if($Dletter$=="L" && #quest==14) goto Npcland_mdk;
			if($Dletter$=="S" && #quest==14) goto Npcland_mdk;

			if($Dletter$=="W" && #quest==12) goto Npcland_mdk;
			if($Dletter$=="I" && #quest==12) goto Npcland_mdk;
			if($Dletter$=="N" && #quest==18) goto Npcland_mdk;
			if($Dletter$=="N" && #quest==18) goto Npcland_mdk;
			if($Dletter$=="E" && #quest==20) goto Npcland_mdk;
			if($Dletter$=="R" && #quest==17) goto Npcland_mdk;

			if($Dletter$=="B" && #quest==18) goto Npcland_mdk;
			if($Dletter$=="S" && #quest==14) goto Npcland_mdk;
			if($Dletter$=="M" && #quest==14) goto Npcland_mdk;
			if($Dletter$=="I" && #quest==12) goto Npcland_mdk;
			if($Dletter$=="T" && #quest==12) goto Npcland_mdk;
			if($Dletter$=="H" && #quest==16) goto Npcland_mdk;

			if($Dletter$=="R" && #quest==17) goto Npcland_mdk;
			if($Dletter$=="A" && #quest==18) goto Npcland_mdk;
			if($Dletter$=="N" && #quest==18) goto Npcland_mdk;
			if($Dletter$=="G" && #quest==18) goto Npcland_mdk;
			if($Dletter$=="E" && #quest==20) goto Npcland_mdk;
			if($Dletter$=="R" && #quest==17) goto Npcland_mdk;

			if($Dletter$=="A" && #quest==18) goto Npcland_mdk;
			if($Dletter$=="M" && #quest==14) goto Npcland_mdk;
			if($Dletter$=="I" && #quest==12) goto Npcland_mdk;
			if($Dletter$=="S" && #quest==14) goto Npcland_mdk;
			if($Dletter$=="T" && #quest==12) goto Npcland_mdk;
			if($Dletter$=="R" && #quest==17) goto Npcland_mdk;

			if($Dletter$=="K" && #quest==15) goto Npcland_mdk;
			if($Dletter$=="N" && #quest==18) goto Npcland_mdk;
			if($Dletter$=="I" && #quest==12) goto Npcland_mdk;
			if($Dletter$=="G" && #quest==18) goto Npcland_mdk;
			if($Dletter$=="H" && #quest==16) goto Npcland_mdk;
			if($Dletter$=="T" && #quest==12) goto Npcland_mdk;

			if($Dletter$=="P" && #quest==14) goto Npcland_mdk;
			if($Dletter$=="R" && #quest==17) goto Npcland_mdk;
			if($Dletter$=="I" && #quest==12) goto Npcland_mdk;
			if($Dletter$=="E" && #quest==20) goto Npcland_mdk;
			if($Dletter$=="S" && #quest==14) goto Npcland_mdk;
			if($Dletter$=="T" && #quest==12) goto Npcland_mdk;

			if($Dletter$=="W" && #quest==12) goto Npcland_mdk;
			if($Dletter$=="I" && #quest==12) goto Npcland_mdk;
			if($Dletter$=="Z" && #quest==16) goto Npcland_mdk;
			if($Dletter$=="A" && #quest==18) goto Npcland_mdk;
			if($Dletter$=="R" && #quest==17) goto Npcland_mdk;
			if($Dletter$=="D" && #quest==19) goto Npcland_mdk;

			if($Dletter$=="N" && #quest==18) goto Npcland_mdk;
			if($Dletter$=="O" && #quest==17) goto Npcland_mdk;
			if($Dletter$=="V" && #quest==12) goto Npcland_mdk;
			if($Dletter$=="I" && #quest==12) goto Npcland_mdk;
			if($Dletter$=="C" && #quest==11) goto Npcland_mdk;
			if($Dletter$=="E" && #quest==20) goto Npcland_mdk;

			if($Dletter$=="D" && #quest==19) goto Npcland_mdk;
			if($Dletter$=="A" && #quest==18) goto Npcland_mdk;
			if($Dletter$=="N" && #quest==18) goto Npcland_mdk;
			if($Dletter$=="C" && #quest==11) goto Npcland_mdk;
			if($Dletter$=="E" && #quest==20) goto Npcland_mdk;
			if($Dletter$=="R" && #quest==17) goto Npcland_mdk;
//end of #quest,#quest+1 variables

			else next;
			mes "^DC143C[Npcland Manager]^000000";
			callfunc "ViewRemovals";
			set #quest,0;
			mes "Minimap markings have been removed and quest status has been reset. Thank you, come again...";
			mes "I will now return you to the main menu";
			next;
			goto Npcland_Main;
		case 2:
			mes "^DC143C[Npcland Manager]^000000";
			mes "I am now returning you to the main menu...";
			next;
			goto Npcland_Main;
		}


Npcland_mdk:
	mes "^DC143C[Npcland Manager]^000000";
	mes "I suggest you start running...";
	close2;
	npctalk "Everyone congratulate "+strcharinfo(0)+" for attempting to cheat";
	sleep2 1000;
	npctalk "Cheaters go BOOM!";
	specialeffect2 501;
	specialeffect2 266;
	sleep2 1000;
	specialeffect2 183;
	percentheal-100,0;
	end;


Npcland_WordChange:
	if(getgmlevel() > 80) goto Npcland_Change;
	else mes "^DC143C[Npcland Manager]^000000";
	mes "Im sorry, but for security purposes...you require a higher GM level to use this function. You will now be returned to the main menu.";
	next;
	goto Npcland_Main;


Npcland_WordCheck:
	if(getgmlevel() > 80) goto Npcland_WordView;
	else mes "^DC143C[Npcland Manager]^000000";
	mes "Im sorry, but for security purposes...you require a higher GM level to use this function. You will now be returned to the main menu.";
	next;
	goto Npcland_Main;


Npcland_WordView:
	mes "^DC143C[Npcland Manager]^000000";
	mes "Hello GM "+strcharinfo(0)+", this weeks word is: "+ $Word$ +". Remember, knowing the word does not negate the fact that you must do the daily quests to gain access to input your guess for the week.";
	next;
	mes "^DC143C[Npcland Manager]^000000";
	mes "Ill now return you to the main menu.";
	next;
	goto Npcland_Main;


Npcland_Change:
	if(gettime(4)==0) goto Npcland_SundayGMChange;
	mes "^DC143C[Npcland Manager]^000000";
	mes "Hello GM "+strcharinfo(0)+", I must inform you that changing the weekly word will nullify any previous saved variables. The change will also be reflected in todays daily letter.";
	next;
	mes "^DC143C[Npcland Manager]^000000";
	mes "Example: If today is Friday and you change the word to *RIVALS* then todays daily will become Letter *L*";
	next;
	mes "^DC143C[Npcland Manager]^000000";
	mes "There will be a serverwide announcement detailing that the weekly word has been changed, what it used to be and who changed it also!";
switch(select("RIVALS","WINNER","BSMITH","RANGER","AMISTR","KNIGHT","PRIEST","WIZARD","NOVICE","DANCER","CANCEL CHANGES")){
	case 1:
		next;
		announce "The weekly word at Npcland has been changed by GM "+strcharinfo(0)+". The old word was "+ $Word$ +".",0;
		sleep2 2000;
		//announce "You may also redo todays daily quest at Npcland",0;
		set $Word$,"RIVALS";
		set $Reset,1;
		if(gettime(4)==1){ set $Letter,1;
		callfunc "Daily Letter";
		next;
		goto Npcland_Main;}
		if(gettime(4)==2){ set $Letter,2;
		callfunc "Daily Letter";
		next;
		goto Npcland_Main;}
		if(gettime(4)==3){ set $Letter,3;
		callfunc "Daily Letter";
		next;
		goto Npcland_Main;}
		if(gettime(4)==4){ set $Letter,4;
		callfunc "Daily Letter";
		next;
		goto Npcland_Main;}
		if(gettime(4)==5){ set $Letter,5;
		callfunc "Daily Letter";
		next;
		goto Npcland_Main;}
		if(gettime(4)==6){ set $Letter,6;
		callfunc "Daily Letter";
		next;
		goto Npcland_Main;}
	case 2:
		next;
		announce "The weekly word at Npcland has been changed from by GM "+strcharinfo(0)+". The old word was "+ $Word$ +".",0;
		sleep2 2000;
		//announce "You may also redo todays daily quest at Npcland",0;
		set $Word$,"WINNER";
		set $Reset,1;
		if(gettime(4)==1){ set $Letter,1;
		callfunc "Daily Letter";
		next;
		goto Npcland_Main;}
		if(gettime(4)==2){ set $Letter,2;
		callfunc "Daily Letter";
		next;
		goto Npcland_Main;}
		if(gettime(4)==3){ set $Letter,3;
		callfunc "Daily Letter";
		next;
		goto Npcland_Main;}
		if(gettime(4)==4){ set $Letter,4;
		callfunc "Daily Letter";
		next;
		goto Npcland_Main;}
		if(gettime(4)==5){ set $Letter,5;
		callfunc "Daily Letter";
		next;
		goto Npcland_Main;}
		if(gettime(4)==6){ set $Letter,6;
		callfunc "Daily Letter";
		next;
		goto Npcland_Main;}
	case 3:
		next;
		announce "The weekly word at Npcland has been changed from by GM "+strcharinfo(0)+". The old word was "+ $Word$ +".",0;
		sleep2 2000;
		//announce "You may also redo todays daily quest at Npcland",0;
		set $Word$,"BSMITH";
		set $Reset,1;
		if(gettime(4)==1){ set $Letter,1;
		callfunc "Daily Letter";
		next;
		goto Npcland_Main;}
		if(gettime(4)==2){ set $Letter,2;
		callfunc "Daily Letter";
		next;
		goto Npcland_Main;}
		if(gettime(4)==3){ set $Letter,3;
		callfunc "Daily Letter";
		next;
		goto Npcland_Main;}
		if(gettime(4)==4){ set $Letter,4;
		callfunc "Daily Letter";
		next;
		goto Npcland_Main;}
		if(gettime(4)==5){ set $Letter,5;
		callfunc "Daily Letter";
		next;
		goto Npcland_Main;}
		if(gettime(4)==6){ set $Letter,6;
		callfunc "Daily Letter";
		next;
		goto Npcland_Main;}
	case 4:
		next;
		announce "The weekly word at Npcland has been changed from by GM "+strcharinfo(0)+". The old word was "+ $Word$ +".",0;
		sleep2 2000;
		//announce "You may also redo todays daily quest at Npcland",0;
		set $Word$,"RANGER";
		set $Reset,1;
		if(gettime(4)==1){ set $Letter,1;
		callfunc "Daily Letter";
		next;
		goto Npcland_Main;}
		if(gettime(4)==2){ set $Letter,2;
		callfunc "Daily Letter";
		next;
		goto Npcland_Main;}
		if(gettime(4)==3){ set $Letter,3;
		callfunc "Daily Letter";
		next;
		goto Npcland_Main;}
		if(gettime(4)==4){ set $Letter,4;
		callfunc "Daily Letter";
		next;
		goto Npcland_Main;}
		if(gettime(4)==5){ set $Letter,5;
		callfunc "Daily Letter";
		next;
		goto Npcland_Main;}
		if(gettime(4)==6){ set $Letter,6;
		callfunc "Daily Letter";
		next;
		goto Npcland_Main;}
	case 5:

function	script	NpclandInit	{
		if(gettime(4)==1){ set $Letter,1;
		return;}
		if(gettime(4)==2){ set $Letter,2;
		return;}
		if(gettime(4)==3){ set $Letter,3;
		return;}
		if(gettime(4)==4){ set $Letter,4;
		return;}
		if(gettime(4)==5){ set $Letter,5;
		return;}
		if(gettime(4)==6){ set $Letter,6;
		return;}
		if(gettime(4)==0){ set $Letter,7;
		return;}
}

function	script	NpclandSSwitch	{
//if(gettime(4)==0) 
switch(rand(10)){
		case 1:
			set $Word$,"RIVALS";
			return;
		case 2:
			set $Word$,"WINNER";
			return;
		case 3:
			set $Word$,"BSMITH";
			return;
		case 4:
			set $Word$,"RANGER";
			return;
		case 5:
			set $Word$,"AMISTR";
			return;
		case 6:
			set $Word$,"KNIGHT";
			return;
		case 7:
			set $Word$,"PRIEST";
			return;
		case 8:
			set $Word$,"WIZARD";
			return;
		case 9:
			set $Word$,"NOVICE";
			return;
		case 10:
			set $Word$,"DANCER";
			return;
		}
}		


function	script	Daily Letter	{
	if ($Letter==1 && $Word$=="RIVALS"){ set $Dletter$,"R";
	return;}
	if ($Letter==2 && $Word$=="RIVALS"){ set $Dletter$,"I";
	return;}
	if ($Letter==3 && $Word$=="RIVALS"){ set $Dletter$,"V";
	return;}
	if ($Letter==4 && $Word$=="RIVALS"){ set $Dletter$,"A";
	return;}
	if ($Letter==5 && $Word$=="RIVALS"){ set $Dletter$,"L";
	return;}
	if ($Letter==6 && $Word$=="RIVALS"){ set $Dletter$,"S";
	return;}

	if ($Letter==1 && $Word$=="WINNER"){ set $Dletter$,"W";
	return;}
